```java
// æ•°æ®è¿ç§»æœåŠ¡
@Service
@Slf4j
public class DataMigrationService {
    
    private final DataSource dataSource;
    private final JdbcTemplate jdbcTemplate;
    private final MigrationHistoryRepository migrationHistoryRepository;
    
    public DataMigrationService(DataSource dataSource,
                              JdbcTemplate jdbcTemplate,
                              MigrationHistoryRepository migrationHistoryRepository) {
        this.dataSource = dataSource;
        this.jdbcTemplate = jdbcTemplate;
        this.migrationHistoryRepository = migrationHistoryRepository;
    }
    
    // å…¨é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»
    @Transactional
    public MigrationResult fullMigration(String sourceDatabase, String targetDatabase) {
        MigrationResult result = new MigrationResult();
        result.setStartTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        
        try {
            log.info("å¼€å§‹å…¨é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»: {} -> {}", sourceDatabase, targetDatabase);
            
            // 1. è¿ç§»ç”¨æˆ·æ•°æ®
            migrateUsers(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, result);
            
            // 2. è¿ç§»AIæ¨¡å‹æ•°æ®
            migrateAIModels(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, result);
            
            // 3. è¿ç§»è¯·æ±‚è®°å½•
            migrateAIRequests(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, result);
            
            result.setStatus(MigrationStatus.COMPLETED);
            log.info("å…¨é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»å®Œæˆ: {}", result);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("å…¨é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»å¤±è´¥", e);
            result.setStatus(MigrationStatus.FAILED);
            result.setErrorMessage(e.getMessage());
        } finally {
            result.setEndTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            saveMigrationHistory(result);
        }
        
        return result;
    }
    
    // å¢é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»
    @Transactional
    public MigrationResult incrementalMigration(String sourceDatabase, 
                                              String targetDatabase,
                                              LocalDateTime since) {
        MigrationResult result = new MigrationResult();
        result.setStartTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        
        try {
            log.info("å¼€å§‹å¢é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»: {} -> {}, æ—¶é—´ç‚¹: {}", 
                    sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, since);
            
            // 1. è¿ç§»æ–°å¢ç”¨æˆ·
            migrateNewUsers(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, since, result);
            
            // 2. è¿ç§»æ›´æ–°çš„AIæ¨¡å‹
            migrateUpdatedModels(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, since, result);
            
            // 3. è¿ç§»æ–°çš„è¯·æ±‚è®°å½•
            migrateNewRequests(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, since, result);
            
            result.setStatus(MigrationStatus.COMPLETED);
            log.info("å¢é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»å®Œæˆ: {}", result);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("å¢é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»å¤±è´¥", e);
            result.setStatus(MigrationStatus.FAILED);
            result.setErrorMessage(e.getMessage());
        } finally {
            result.setEndTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            saveMigrationHistory(result);
        }
        
        return result;
    }
    
    // æ•°æ®è¿ç§»éªŒè¯
    public MigrationValidationResult validateMigration(String sourceDatabase, 
                                                     String targetDatabase) {
        MigrationValidationResult validationResult = new MigrationValidationResult();
        
        try {
            // 1. éªŒè¯ç”¨æˆ·æ•°æ®ä¸€è‡´æ€§
            validateUserData(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, validationResult);
            
            // 2. éªŒè¯AIæ¨¡å‹æ•°æ®ä¸€è‡´æ€§
            validateAIModelData(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, validationResult);
            
            // 3. éªŒè¯è¯·æ±‚è®°å½•ä¸€è‡´æ€§
            validateAIRequestData(sourceDatabase, targetDatabase, validationResult);
            
            validationResult.setValid(validationResult.getErrors().isEmpty());
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("æ•°æ®è¿ç§»éªŒè¯å¤±è´¥", e);
            validationResult.addError("éªŒè¯è¿‡ç¨‹å¼‚å¸¸: " + e.getMessage());
            validationResult.setValid(false);
        }
        
        return validationResult;
    }
    
    private void migrateUsers(String sourceDatabase, String targetDatabase, 
                            MigrationResult result) {
        String sql = "INSERT INTO " + targetDatabase + ".users " +
                    "SELECT * FROM " + sourceDatabase + ".users " +
                    "WHERE created_at > ?";
        
        int count = jdbcTemplate.update(sql, result.getLastMigrationTime());
        result.setUsersMigrated(count);
        log.info("è¿ç§»ç”¨æˆ·æ•°æ®: {} æ¡è®°å½•", count);
    }
    
    private void migrateAIModels(String sourceDatabase, String targetDatabase,
                               MigrationResult result) {
        // ç±»ä¼¼ç”¨æˆ·è¿ç§»é€»è¾‘
    }
    
    private void migrateAIRequests(String sourceDatabase, String targetDatabase,
                                 MigrationResult result) {
        // ç±»ä¼¼ç”¨æˆ·è¿ç§»é€»è¾‘
    }
    
    private void saveMigrationHistory(MigrationResult result) {
        MigrationHistory history = new MigrationHistory();
        history.setSourceDatabase(result.getSourceDatabase());
        history.setTargetDatabase(result.getTargetDatabase());
        history.setMigrationType(result.getMigrationType());
        history.setStatus(result.getStatus());
        history.setRecordsMigrated(result.getTotalRecords());
        history.setStartTime(result.getStartTime());
        history.setEndTime(result.getEndTime());
        history.setErrorMessage(result.getErrorMessage());
        
        migrationHistoryRepository.save(history);
    }
}

// åœ¨çº¿æ•°æ®è¿ç§»ï¼ˆé›¶åœæœºï¼‰
@Service
@Slf4j
public class OnlineDataMigrationService {
    
    private final DataSource sourceDataSource;
    private final DataSource targetDataSource;
    private final DualWriteService dualWriteService;
    
    public OnlineDataMigrationService(@Qualifier("sourceDataSource") DataSource sourceDataSource,
                                    @Qualifier("targetDataSource") DataSource targetDataSource,
                                    DualWriteService dualWriteService) {
        this.sourceDataSource = sourceDataSource;
        this.targetDataSource = targetDataSource;
        this.dualWriteService = dualWriteService;
    }
    
    // åœ¨çº¿è¿ç§»æµç¨‹
    public void performOnlineMigration(String migrationPlanId) {
        try {
            // 1. å‡†å¤‡é˜¶æ®µ
            prepareMigration(migrationPlanId);
            
            // 2. å¼€å¯åŒå†™
            dualWriteService.enableDualWrite();
            
            // 3. å…¨é‡æ•°æ®è¿ç§»
            migrateFullData();
            
            // 4. å¢é‡æ•°æ®è¿½èµ¶
            migrateIncrementalData();
            
            // 5. æ•°æ®éªŒè¯
            validateDataConsistency();
            
            // 6. æµé‡åˆ‡æ¢
            switchTraffic();
            
            // 7. æ¸…ç†æ—§æ•°æ®
            cleanupOldData();
            
            log.info("åœ¨çº¿æ•°æ®è¿ç§»å®Œæˆ: {}", migrationPlanId);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("åœ¨çº¿æ•°æ®è¿ç§»å¤±è´¥: {}", migrationPlanId, e);
            rollbackMigration(migrationPlanId);
        }
    }
```

### 9.5.3 ç‰ˆæœ¬å›æ»šæ–¹æ¡ˆ

```sql
-- æ•°æ®åº“ç‰ˆæœ¬å›æ»šè„šæœ¬

-- R1__Rollback_initial_schema.sql
-- å›æ»šåˆ°åˆå§‹ç‰ˆæœ¬

-- R2__Rollback_tenant_isolation.sql
-- å›æ»šå¤šç§Ÿæˆ·æ”¯æŒ

-- R3__Rollback_ai_models.sql
-- å›æ»šAIæ¨¡å‹ç›¸å…³è¡¨
```

```java
// ç‰ˆæœ¬å›æ»šæœåŠ¡
@Service
@Slf4j
public class VersionRollbackService {
    
    private final Flyway flyway;
    private final MigrationHistoryRepository migrationHistoryRepository;
    private final DatabaseBackupService backupService;
    
    public VersionRollbackService(Flyway flyway,
                                MigrationHistoryRepository migrationHistoryRepository,
                                DatabaseBackupService backupService) {
        this.flyway = flyway;
        this.migrationHistoryRepository = migrationHistoryRepository;
        this.backupService = backupService;
    }
    
    // æ•°æ®åº“ç‰ˆæœ¬å›æ»š
    @Transactional
    public RollbackResult rollbackToVersion(String targetVersion, boolean createBackup) {
        RollbackResult result = new RollbackResult();
        result.setStartTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        
        try {
            log.info("å¼€å§‹å›æ»šåˆ°ç‰ˆæœ¬: {}", targetVersion);
            
            // 1. åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½
            if (createBackup) {
                String backupId = backupService.createBackup("rollback_" + targetVersion);
                result.setBackupId(backupId);
            }
            
            // 2. æ‰§è¡Œå›æ»š
            int rolledBackMigrations = flyway.rollbackToVersion(targetVersion);
            result.setRolledBackMigrations(rolledBackMigrations);
            
            // 3. éªŒè¯å›æ»šç»“æœ
            boolean success = validateRollback(targetVersion);
            result.setSuccess(success);
            
            if (success) {
                log.info("ç‰ˆæœ¬å›æ»šæˆåŠŸ: {} -> {}", getCurrentVersion(), targetVersion);
            } else {
                log.error("ç‰ˆæœ¬å›æ»šéªŒè¯å¤±è´¥");
            }
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("ç‰ˆæœ¬å›æ»šå¤±è´¥", e);
            result.setSuccess(false);
            result.setErrorMessage(e.getMessage());
            
            // å°è¯•æ¢å¤å¤‡ä»½
            if (createBackup && result.getBackupId() != null) {
                restoreFromBackup(result.getBackupId());
            }
        } finally {
            result.setEndTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            saveRollbackHistory(result);
        }
        
        return result;
    }
    
    // æ•°æ®å›æ»šï¼ˆä¸šåŠ¡æ•°æ®ï¼‰
    @Transactional
    public DataRollbackResult rollbackData(LocalDateTime targetTime, 
                                         Set<String> tablesToRollback) {
        DataRollbackResult result = new DataRollbackResult();
        result.setTargetTime(targetTime);
        
        try {
            log.info("å¼€å§‹æ•°æ®å›æ»šåˆ°æ—¶é—´ç‚¹: {}", targetTime);
            
            // 1. å¤‡ä»½å½“å‰æ•°æ®
            String backupId = backupService.createBackup("data_rollback_" + 
                targetTime.format(DateTimeFormatter.ISO_LOCAL_DATE_TIME));
            result.setBackupId(backupId);
            
            // 2. æ‰§è¡Œæ•°æ®å›æ»š
            for (String tableName : tablesToRollback) {
                int affectedRows = rollbackTableData(tableName, targetTime);
                result.addTableResult(tableName, affectedRows);
            }
            
            // 3. éªŒè¯æ•°æ®ä¸€è‡´æ€§
            boolean consistent = validateDataConsistency(targetTime, tablesToRollback);
            result.setSuccess(consistent);
            
            log.info("æ•°æ®å›æ»šå®Œæˆ: {}", result);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("æ•°æ®å›æ»šå¤±è´¥", e);
            result.setSuccess(false);
            result.setErrorMessage(e.getMessage());
            
            // æ¢å¤å¤‡ä»½
            if (result.getBackupId() != null) {
                restoreFromBackup(result.getBackupId());
            }
        }
        
        return result;
    }
    
    // ç´§æ€¥å›æ»šæµç¨‹
    public EmergencyRollbackResult emergencyRollback(String rollbackPlanId) {
        EmergencyRollbackResult result = new EmergencyRollbackResult();
        
        try {
            log.warn("æ‰§è¡Œç´§æ€¥å›æ»š: {}", rollbackPlanId);
            
            // 1. åœæ­¢åº”ç”¨æœåŠ¡
            stopApplicationServices();
            
            // 2. æ¢å¤æœ€è¿‘å¤‡ä»½
            String latestBackup = findLatestBackup();
            restoreFromBackup(latestBackup);
            
            // 3. éªŒè¯æ¢å¤ç»“æœ
            boolean recovered = validateRecovery();
            
            // 4. é‡å¯åº”ç”¨æœåŠ¡
            startApplicationServices();
            
            result.setSuccess(recovered);
            result.setBackupUsed(latestBackup);
            result.setRecoveryTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            
            log.info("ç´§æ€¥å›æ»šå®Œæˆ: {}", result);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("ç´§æ€¥å›æ»šå¤±è´¥", e);
            result.setSuccess(false);
            result.setErrorMessage(e.getMessage());
        }
        
        return result;
    }
    
    private int rollbackTableData(String tableName, LocalDateTime targetTime) {
        // ä½¿ç”¨æ—¶é—´ç‚¹æ¢å¤æˆ–é€»è¾‘å›æ»š
        // è¿™é‡Œç®€åŒ–ä¸ºè¿”å›å½±å“è¡Œæ•°
        return jdbcTemplate.update(
            "DELETE FROM " + tableName + " WHERE created_at > ?", 
            targetTime
        );
    }
    
    private boolean validateRollback(String targetVersion) {
        String currentVersion = getCurrentVersion();
        return targetVersion.equals(currentVersion);
    }
    
    private String getCurrentVersion() {
        return flyway.info().current().getVersion().toString();
    }
    
    private void saveRollbackHistory(RollbackResult result) {
        // ä¿å­˜å›æ»šå†å²è®°å½•
    }
    
    private void stopApplicationServices() {
        // åœæ­¢åº”ç”¨æœåŠ¡é€»è¾‘
    }
    
    private void startApplicationServices() {
        // å¯åŠ¨åº”ç”¨æœåŠ¡é€»è¾‘
    }
    
    private String findLatestBackup() {
        // æŸ¥æ‰¾æœ€æ–°å¤‡ä»½
        return backupService.findLatestBackup();
    }
    
    private void restoreFromBackup(String backupId) {
        backupService.restoreBackup(backupId);
    }
    
    private boolean validateDataConsistency(LocalDateTime targetTime, Set<String> tables) {
        // éªŒè¯æ•°æ®ä¸€è‡´æ€§é€»è¾‘
        return true;
    }
    
    private boolean validateRecovery() {
        // éªŒè¯æ¢å¤ç»“æœ
        return true;
    }
}

```

### 9.5.4 æ•°æ®è´¨é‡ç›‘æ§

```sql
-- æ•°æ®è´¨é‡ç›‘æ§è¡¨
CREATE TABLE data_quality_metrics (
    id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_value DECIMAL(15,4) NOT NULL,
    threshold_value DECIMAL(15,4),
    severity severity_level NOT NULL DEFAULT 'info',
    check_time TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(metric_name, table_name, check_time)
);

CREATE TYPE severity_level AS ENUM (
    'info',
    'warning',
    'error',
    'critical'
);

-- æ•°æ®è´¨é‡è§„åˆ™è¡¨
CREATE TABLE data_quality_rules (
    id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    rule_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    rule_type rule_type NOT NULL,
    table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    rule_expression TEXT NOT NULL,
    severity severity_level NOT NULL DEFAULT 'error',
    enabled BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
    description TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TYPE rule_type AS ENUM (
    'completeness',    -- å®Œæ•´æ€§
    'accuracy',        -- å‡†ç¡®æ€§  
    'consistency',     -- ä¸€è‡´æ€§
    'timeliness',      -- åŠæ—¶æ€§
    'validity',        -- æœ‰æ•ˆæ€§
    'uniqueness'       -- å”¯ä¸€æ€§
);

-- æ•°æ®è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥è§†å›¾
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW data_quality_dashboard AS
SELECT 
    table_name,
    metric_name,
    AVG(metric_value) as avg_value,
    MIN(metric_value) as min_value,
    MAX(metric_value) as max_value,
    COUNT(*) as check_count,
    SUM(CASE WHEN metric_value > threshold_value THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as violation_count
FROM data_quality_metrics
WHERE check_time >= NOW() - INTERVAL '7 days'
GROUP BY table_name, metric_name
ORDER BY table_name, metric_name;

```

```java
// æ•°æ®è´¨é‡ç›‘æ§æœåŠ¡
@Service
@Slf4j
public class DataQualityMonitorService {
    
    private final JdbcTemplate jdbcTemplate;
    private final DataQualityRuleRepository ruleRepository;
    private final DataQualityMetricsRepository metricsRepository;
    private final AlertService alertService;
    
    public DataQualityMonitorService(JdbcTemplate jdbcTemplate,
                                   DataQualityRuleRepository ruleRepository,
                                   DataQualityMetricsRepository metricsRepository,
                                   AlertService alertService) {
        this.jdbcTemplate = jdbcTemplate;
        this.ruleRepository = ruleRepository;
        this.metricsRepository = metricsRepository;
        this.alertService = alertService;
    }
    
    // æ‰§è¡Œæ•°æ®è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥
    @Scheduled(cron = "0 0 2 * * ?") // æ¯å¤©å‡Œæ™¨2ç‚¹æ‰§è¡Œ
    public void performDataQualityCheck() {
        log.info("å¼€å§‹æ•°æ®è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥");
        
        List<DataQualityRule> rules = ruleRepository.findByEnabledTrue();
        
        for (DataQualityRule rule : rules) {
            try {
                DataQualityMetric metric = executeQualityRule(rule);
                metricsRepository.save(metric);
                
                // æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦è§¦å‘å‘Šè­¦
                if (metric.isViolation()) {
                    triggerQualityAlert(rule, metric);
                }
                
            } catch (Exception e) {
                log.error("æ‰§è¡Œæ•°æ®è´¨é‡è§„åˆ™å¤±è´¥: {}", rule.getRuleName(), e);
            }
        }
        
        log.info("æ•°æ®è´¨é‡æ£€æŸ¥å®Œæˆ");
    }
    
    // å®æ—¶æ•°æ®è´¨é‡ç›‘æ§
    @EventListener
    public void monitorRealTimeData(QualityCheckEvent event) {
        String tableName = event.getTableName();
        String operation = event.getOperation();
        
        // è·å–ç›¸å…³è´¨é‡è§„åˆ™
        List<DataQualityRule> rules = ruleRepository
            .findByTableNameAndEnabledTrue(tableName);
        
        for (DataQualityRule rule : rules) {
            if (shouldCheckRule(rule, operation)) {
                DataQualityMetric metric = executeQualityRule(rule);
                metricsRepository.save(metric);
                
                if (metric.isViolation()) {
                    triggerRealTimeAlert(rule, metric);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // æ•°æ®è´¨é‡æŠ¥å‘Šç”Ÿæˆ
    public DataQualityReport generateQualityReport(LocalDate startDate, LocalDate endDate) {
        DataQualityReport report = new DataQualityReport();
        report.setPeriod(startDate + " è‡³ " + endDate);
        report.setGeneratedAt(LocalDateTime.now());
        
        // è®¡ç®—æ€»ä½“è´¨é‡åˆ†æ•°
        BigDecimal overallScore = calculateOverallQualityScore(startDate, endDate);
        report.setOverallScore(overallScore);
        
        // æŒ‰è¡¨ç»Ÿè®¡è´¨é‡æŒ‡æ ‡
        Map<String, TableQualityStats> tableStats = calculateTableQualityStats(startDate, endDate);
        report.setTableStats(tableStats);
        
        // è¯†åˆ«è´¨é‡é—®é¢˜
        List<QualityIssue> issues = identifyQualityIssues(startDate, endDate);
        report.setQualityIssues(issues);
        
        // ç”Ÿæˆæ”¹è¿›å»ºè®®
        List<QualityImprovement> improvements = generateImprovementSuggestions(issues);
        report.setImprovements(improvements);
        
        return report;
    }
    
    private DataQualityMetric executeQualityRule(DataQualityRule rule) {
        DataQualityMetric metric = new DataQualityMetric();
        metric.setRuleName(rule.getRuleName());
        metric.setTableName(rule.getTableName());
        metric.setSeverity(rule.getSeverity());
        
        try {
            // æ‰§è¡ŒSQLè§„åˆ™è¡¨è¾¾å¼
            BigDecimal value = jdbcTemplate.queryForObject(
                rule.getRuleExpression(), BigDecimal.class);
            
            metric.setMetricValue(value);
            metric.setThresholdValue(rule.getThresholdValue());
            metric.setCheckTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            metric.setViolation(value.compareTo(rule.getThresholdValue()) > 0);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("æ‰§è¡Œæ•°æ®è´¨é‡è§„åˆ™SQLå¤±è´¥: {}", rule.getRuleExpression(), e);
            metric.setError(true);
            metric.setErrorMessage(e.getMessage());
        }
        
        return metric;
    }
    
    private void triggerQualityAlert(DataQualityRule rule, DataQualityMetric metric) {
        Alert alert = new Alert();
        alert.setType(AlertType.DATA_QUALITY);
        alert.setTitle("æ•°æ®è´¨é‡å‘Šè­¦: " + rule.getRuleName());
        alert.setMessage(String.format(
            "è¡¨ %s çš„æ•°æ®è´¨é‡è§„åˆ™ %s è§¦å‘å‘Šè­¦ï¼Œå½“å‰å€¼: %s, é˜ˆå€¼: %s",
            rule.getTableName(), rule.getRuleName(), 
            metric.getMetricValue(), rule.getThresholdValue()));
        alert.setSeverity(rule.getSeverity());
        alert.setMetadata(Map.of(
            "ruleName", rule.getRuleName(),
            "tableName", rule.getTableName(),
            "metricValue", metric.getMetricValue().toString(),
            "thresholdValue", rule.getThresholdValue().toString()
        ));
        
        alertService.sendAlert(alert);
    }
    
    private boolean shouldCheckRule(DataQualityRule rule, String operation) {
        // æ ¹æ®æ“ä½œç±»å‹å†³å®šæ˜¯å¦æ£€æŸ¥è§„åˆ™
        return true;
    }
    
    private void triggerRealTimeAlert(DataQualityRule rule, DataQualityMetric metric) {
        // å®æ—¶å‘Šè­¦é€»è¾‘
    }
    
    private BigDecimal calculateOverallQualityScore(LocalDate startDate, LocalDate endDate) {
        // è®¡ç®—æ€»ä½“è´¨é‡åˆ†æ•°
        return BigDecimal.valueOf(95.5);
    }
    
    private Map<String, TableQualityStats> calculateTableQualityStats(LocalDate startDate, LocalDate endDate) {
        // è®¡ç®—è¡¨çº§åˆ«è´¨é‡ç»Ÿè®¡
        return new HashMap<>();
    }
    
    private List<QualityIssue> identifyQualityIssues(LocalDate startDate, LocalDate endDate) {
        // è¯†åˆ«è´¨é‡é—®é¢˜
        return new ArrayList<>();
    }
    
    private List<QualityImprovement> generateImprovementSuggestions(List<QualityIssue> issues) {
        // ç”Ÿæˆæ”¹è¿›å»ºè®®
        return new ArrayList<>();
    }
}
```

```scss
@mixin apply-theme($theme) {
  @if map-has-key($color-system, $theme) {
    $theme-colors: map-get($color-system, $theme);
    
    --color-primary: #{map-get($theme-colors, primary)};
    --color-secondary: #{map-get($theme-colors, secondary)};
    --color-light: #{map-get($theme-colors, light)};
    --color-dark: #{map-get($theme-colors, dark)};
    --color-accent: #{map-get($theme-colors, accent)};
    --color-border: #{map-get($theme-colors, border)};
    --color-shadow: #{map-get($theme-colors, shadow)};
    --gradient: #{map-get($theme-colors, gradient)};
  }
}

@mixin text-color($type: primary) {
  @if map-has-key($text-colors, $type) {
    color: map-get($text-colors, $type);
  } @else {
    color: map-get($text-colors, primary);
  }
}

@mixin bg-color($type: primary) {
  @if map-has-key($background-colors, $type) {
    background-color: map-get($background-colors, $type);
  } @else {
    background-color: map-get($background-colors, primary);
  }
}

@mixin border-color($type: default) {
  @if map-has-key($border-colors, $type) {
    border-color: map-get($border-colors, $type);
  } @else {
    border-color: map-get($border-colors, default);
  }
}

@mixin shadow($type: default) {
  @if map-has-key($shadows, $type) {
    box-shadow: map-get($shadows, $type);
  } @else {
    box-shadow: map-get($shadows, default);
  }
}

// åŠŸèƒ½ç±»ç”Ÿæˆå™¨
@each $name, $colors in $color-system {
  .theme-#{$name} {
    @include apply-theme($name);
  }
  
  .text-#{$name} {
    color: map-get($colors, primary) !important;
  }
  
  .bg-#{$name} {
    background-color: map-get($colors, primary) !important;
  }
  
  .border-#{$name} {
    border-color: map-get($colors, primary) !important;
  }
  
  .shadow-#{$name} {
    box-shadow: 0 4px 6px -1px map-get($colors, shadow) !important;
  }
}

```

### 11.1.2 æ™ºèƒ½å¯¼èˆªæ ç»„ä»¶

```plaintext
<!-- components/navigation/IntelligentNavBar.vue -->
<template>
  <div class="intelligent-nav-bar" :class="`theme-${currentTheme}`">
    <!-- åŠŸèƒ½åˆ†ç±»èœå•æ  -->
    <div class="function-category-bar">
      <div class="category-container">
        <div
          v-for="category in categories"
          :key="category.id"
          class="category-item"
          :class="{ active: currentCategory === category.id }"
          @click="switchCategory(category.id)"
          @mouseenter="handleCategoryHover(category)"
        >
          <div class="category-icon">
            <i :class="category.icon"></i>
          </div>
          <span class="category-name">{{ category.name }}</span>
          <div class="category-indicator"></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- ç”¨æˆ·æ“ä½œåŒº -->
      <div class="user-actions">
        <div class="search-box">
          <i class="icon-search"></i>
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="æ™ºèƒ½æœç´¢..."
            v-model="searchQuery"
            @focus="showSearchSuggestions = true"
          />
          <transition name="slide-down">
            <div
              v-if="showSearchSuggestions && searchQuery"
              class="search-suggestions"
            >
              <div
                v-for="suggestion in searchSuggestions"
                :key="suggestion.id"
                class="suggestion-item"
                @click="handleSuggestionSelect(suggestion)"
              >
                <i :class="suggestion.icon"></i>
                <span>{{ suggestion.text }}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </transition>
        </div>
        
        <div class="user-menu">
          <div class="user-avatar" @click="toggleUserMenu">
            <img :src="user.avatar" :alt="user.name" />
          </div>
          <transition name="slide-down">
            <div v-if="showUserMenu" class="user-dropdown">
              <div class="user-info">
                <div class="user-name">{{ user.name }}</div>
                <div class="user-role">{{ user.role }}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="menu-items">
                <div
                  v-for="item in userMenuItems"
                  :key="item.id"
                  class="menu-item"
                  @click="handleUserMenuClick(item)"
                >
                  <i :class="item.icon"></i>
                  <span>{{ item.label }}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </transition>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- é¢åŒ…å±‘å¯¼èˆªæ  -->
    <div class="breadcrumb-bar">
      <div class="breadcrumb-container">
        <nav class="breadcrumb">
          <span
            v-for="(item, index) in breadcrumbs"
            :key="item.path"
            class="breadcrumb-item"
          >
            <span
              v-if="index === breadcrumbs.length - 1"
              class="breadcrumb-current"
            >
              {{ item.name }}
            </span>
            <router-link
              v-else
              :to="item.path"
              class="breadcrumb-link"
            >
              {{ item.name }}
            </router-link>
            <span
              v-if="index < breadcrumbs.length - 1"
              class="breadcrumb-separator"
            >
              <i class="icon-chevron-right"></i>
            </span>
          </span>
        </nav>
        
        <!-- å¿«æ·æ“ä½œ -->
        <div class="quick-actions">
          <button
            v-for="action in quickActions"
            :key="action.id"
            class="quick-action-btn"
            :class="`theme-${action.theme}`"
            @click="handleQuickAction(action)"
          >
            <i :class="action.icon"></i>
            <span>{{ action.label }}</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡æç¤º -->
    <transition name="fade">
      <div
        v-if="contextHint"
        class="context-hint"
        :class="`theme-${contextHint.theme}`"
      >
        <i :class="contextHint.icon"></i>
        <span>{{ contextHint.message }}</span>
        <button class="hint-close" @click="closeContextHint">
          <i class="icon-close"></i>
        </button>
      </div>
    </transition>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, computed, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue'
import { useRoute, useRouter } from 'vue-router'

// Props
const props = defineProps({
  user: {
    type: Object,
    required: true
  }
})

// è·¯ç”±ç›¸å…³
const route = useRoute()
const router = useRouter()

// å“åº”å¼æ•°æ®
const currentCategory = ref('menu')
const searchQuery = ref('')
const showSearchSuggestions = ref(false)
const showUserMenu = ref(false)
const contextHint = ref(null)

// åŠŸèƒ½åˆ†ç±»æ•°æ®
const categories = ref([
  {
    id: 'menu',
    name: 'æ™ºèƒ½èœå•',
    icon: 'icon-layout',
    theme: 'menu',
    path: '/intelligent-menu'
  },
  {
    id: 'form',
    name: 'æ™ºèƒ½è¡¨å•',
    icon: 'icon-form',
    theme: 'form',
    path: '/intelligent-form'
  },
  {
    id: 'knowledge',
    name: 'çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±',
    icon: 'icon-brain',
    theme: 'knowledge',
    path: '/knowledge-graph'
  },
  {
    id: 'ai',
    name: 'AIæœåŠ¡',
    icon: 'icon-ai',
    theme: 'ai',
    path: '/ai-services'
  },
  {
    id: 'data',
    name: 'æ•°æ®æœåŠ¡',
    icon: 'icon-database',
    theme: 'data',
    path: '/data-services'
  },
  {
    id: 'system',
    name: 'ç³»ç»Ÿç®¡ç†',
    icon: 'icon-settings',
    theme: 'system',
    path: '/system'
  }
])

// æœç´¢å»ºè®®
const searchSuggestions = computed(() => {
  if (!searchQuery.value) return []
  
  const query = searchQuery.value.toLowerCase()
  const allSuggestions = [
    { id: 1, text: 'åˆ›å»ºæ–°èœå•', icon: 'icon-plus', type: 'menu', path: '/intelligent-menu/create' },
    { id: 2, text: 'è®¾è®¡è¡¨å•æ¨¡æ¿', icon: 'icon-form', type: 'form', path: '/intelligent-form/templates' },
    { id: 3, text: 'çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±æœç´¢', icon: 'icon-search', type: 'knowledge', path: '/knowledge-graph/search' },
    { id: 4, text: 'AIæ¨¡å‹ç®¡ç†', icon: 'icon-ai', type: 'ai', path: '/ai-services/models' },
    { id: 5, text: 'æ•°æ®çœ‹æ¿', icon: 'icon-chart', type: 'data', path: '/data-services/dashboard' }
  ]
  
  return allSuggestions.filter(suggestion => 
    suggestion.text.toLowerCase().includes(query)
  )
})

// ç”¨æˆ·èœå•é¡¹
const userMenuItems = ref([
  { id: 1, label: 'ä¸ªäººè®¾ç½®', icon: 'icon-user', action: 'profile' },
  { id: 2, label: 'æ¶ˆæ¯ä¸­å¿ƒ', icon: 'icon-bell', action: 'notifications' },
  { id: 3, label: 'ä½¿ç”¨ç»Ÿè®¡', icon: 'icon-chart', action: 'statistics' },
  { id: 4, label: 'å¸®åŠ©æ–‡æ¡£', icon: 'icon-help', action: 'help' },
  { id: 5, label: 'é€€å‡ºç™»å½•', icon: 'icon-logout', action: 'logout' }
])

// å¿«æ·æ“ä½œ
const quickActions = ref([
  { id: 1, label: 'æ–°å»º', icon: 'icon-plus', theme: 'menu', action: 'create' },
  { id: 2, label: 'å¯¼å…¥', icon: 'icon-upload', theme: 'form', action: 'import' },
  { id: 3, label: 'å¯¼å‡º', icon: 'icon-download', theme: 'data', action: 'export' },
  { id: 4, label: 'åˆ·æ–°', icon: 'icon-refresh', theme: 'system', action: 'refresh' }
])

// è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
const currentTheme = computed(() => {
  return currentCategory.value
})

const breadcrumbs = computed(() => {
  const matched = route.matched.filter(record => record.meta?.breadcrumb)
  return matched.map(record => ({
    name: record.meta.breadcrumb,
    path: record.path
  }))
})

// æ–¹æ³•
const switchCategory = (categoryId) => {
  currentCategory.value = categoryId
  const category = categories.value.find(c => c.id === categoryId)
  if (category) {
    router.push(category.path)
  }
  showContextHint({
    message: `å·²åˆ‡æ¢åˆ°${category?.name}åŠŸèƒ½`,
    theme: categoryId,
    icon: 'icon-check'
  })
}

const handleCategoryHover = (category) => {
  // æ‚¬åœæ•ˆæœå¤„ç†
}

const handleSuggestionSelect = (suggestion) => {
  router.push(suggestion.path)
  showSearchSuggestions.value = false
  searchQuery.value = ''
}

const toggleUserMenu = () => {
  showUserMenu.value = !showUserMenu.value
}

const handleUserMenuClick = (item) => {
  switch (item.action) {
    case 'profile':
      router.push('/profile')
      break
    case 'logout':
      handleLogout()
      break
    // å…¶ä»–æ“ä½œå¤„ç†
  }
  showUserMenu.value = false
}

const handleQuickAction = (action) => {
  // å¤„ç†å¿«æ·æ“ä½œ
  console.log('Quick action:', action)
}

const showContextHint = (hint) => {
  contextHint.value = hint
  setTimeout(() => {
    closeContextHint()
  }, 3000)
}

const closeContextHint = () => {
  contextHint.value = null
}

const handleLogout = () => {
  // é€€å‡ºç™»å½•é€»è¾‘
  console.log('Logout')
}

const handleClickOutside = (event) => {
  const userMenu = document.querySelector('.user-menu')
  const searchBox = document.querySelector('.search-box')
  
  if (userMenu && !userMenu.contains(event.target)) {
    showUserMenu.value = false
  }
  
  if (searchBox && !searchBox.contains(event.target)) {
    showSearchSuggestions.value = false
  }
}

// ç”Ÿå‘½å‘¨æœŸ
onMounted(() => {
  document.addEventListener('click', handleClickOutside)
  // æ ¹æ®å½“å‰è·¯ç”±è®¾ç½®åˆ†ç±»
  const currentPath = route.path
  const matchedCategory = categories.value.find(category => 
    currentPath.startsWith(category.path)
  )
  if (matchedCategory) {
    currentCategory.value = matchedCategory.id
  }
})

onUnmounted(() => {
  document.removeEventListener('click', handleClickOutside)
})
</script>
```

## 11.2 æ™ºèƒ½åŠŸèƒ½å¡ç‰‡ç³»ç»Ÿ

### 11.2.1 å¡ç‰‡ç»„ä»¶å·¥å‚

```plaintext
<!-- components/cards/CardFactory.vue -->
<template>
  <component
    :is="cardComponent"
    v-bind="cardProps"
    @action="handleCardAction"
  />
</template>

<script setup>
import { computed } from 'vue'

// Props
const props = defineProps({
  type: {
    type: String,
    required: true,
    validator: (value) => [
      'statistic',
      'action',
      'data',
      'chart',
      'list',
      'progress',
      'status',
      'ai'
    ].includes(value)
  },
  theme: {
    type: String,
    default: 'system',
    validator: (value) => [
      'menu', 'form', 'knowledge', 'ai', 'data', 'system'
    ].includes(value)
  },
  data: {
    type: Object,
    required: true
  },
  config: {
    type: Object,
    default: () => ({})
  }
})

// Emits
const emit = defineEmits(['action'])

// å¡ç‰‡ç»„ä»¶æ˜ å°„
const cardComponents = {
  statistic: () => import('./StatisticCard.vue'),
  action: () => import('./ActionCard.vue'),
  data: () => import('./DataCard.vue'),
  chart: () => import('./ChartCard.vue'),
  list: () => import('./ListCard.vue'),
  progress: () => import('./ProgressCard.vue'),
  status: () => import('./StatusCard.vue'),
  ai: () => import('./AICard.vue')
}

// è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
const cardComponent = computed(() => {
  return cardComponents[props.type]
})

const cardProps = computed(() => ({
  theme: props.theme,
  data: props.data,
  config: props.config
}))

// æ–¹æ³•
const handleCardAction = (action) => {
  emit('action', action)
}
</script>

```

```plaintext
<!-- components/cards/StatisticCard.vue -->
<template>
  <div class="statistic-card" :class="`theme-${theme}`">
    <div class="card-header">
      <div class="header-content">
        <div class="title-section">
          <i :class="data.icon" class="card-icon"></i>
          <div class="title-group">
            <h3 class="card-title">{{ data.title }}</h3>
            <p class="card-subtitle" v-if="data.subtitle">
              {{ data.subtitle }}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="header-actions" v-if="data.actions">
          <button
            v-for="action in data.actions"
            :key="action.id"
            class="action-btn"
            @click="handleAction(action)"
          >
            <i :class="action.icon"></i>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="card-body">
      <div class="statistic-content">
        <div class="main-value">
          <span class="value">{{ formattedValue }}</span>
          <span class="unit" v-if="data.unit">{{ data.unit }}</span>
        </div>
        
        <div class="comparison" v-if="data.comparison">
          <div class="trend" :class="data.comparison.trend">
            <i :class="trendIcon"></i>
            <span class="trend-value">
              {{ Math.abs(data.comparison.value) }}%
            </span>
          </div>
          <span class="comparison-label">{{ data.comparison.label }}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="progress-container" v-if="data.progress">
        <div class="progress-bar">
          <div
            class="progress-fill"
            :style="{ width: `${data.progress.percentage}%` }"
          ></div>
        </div>
        <div class="progress-label">
          <span>{{ data.progress.label }}</span>
          <span>{{ data.progress.percentage }}%</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="card-footer" v-if="data.footer">
      <div class="footer-content">
        <span class="footer-text">{{ data.footer.text }}</span>
        <button
          v-if="data.footer.action"
          class="footer-btn"
          @click="handleAction(data.footer.action)"
        >
          {{ data.footer.action.label }}
          <i :class="data.footer.action.icon"></i>
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- è£…é¥°å…ƒç´  -->
    <div class="card-decoration">
      <div class="decoration-circle circle-1"></div>
      <div class="decoration-circle circle-2"></div>
      <div class="decoration-wave"></div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
import { computed } from 'vue'

// Props
const props = defineProps({
  theme: {
    type: String,
    default: 'system'
  },
  data: {
    type: Object,
    required: true
  },
  config: {
    type: Object,
    default: () => ({})
  }
})

// Emits
const emit = defineEmits(['action'])

// è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
const formattedValue = computed(() => {
  const value = props.data.value
  if (typeof value === 'number') {
    return new Intl.NumberFormat().format(value)
  }
  return value
})

const trendIcon = computed(() => {
  const trend = props.data.comparison?.trend
  return trend === 'up' ? 'icon-trend-up' : 'icon-trend-down'
})

// æ–¹æ³•
const handleAction = (action) => {
  emit('action', action)
}
</script>
```

### 11.2.2 å¡ç‰‡ç½‘æ ¼å¸ƒå±€ç³»ç»Ÿ

```plaintext
<!-- components/layout/CardGridSystem.vue -->
<template>
  <div class="card-grid-system">
    <!-- å¸ƒå±€é€‰æ‹©å™¨ -->
    <div class="layout-controls" v-if="showControls">
      <div class="layout-options">
        <button
          v-for="layout in layoutOptions"
          :key="layout.id"
          class="layout-btn"
          :class="{ active: currentLayout === layout.id }"
          @click="switchLayout(layout.id)"
        >
          <i :class="layout.icon"></i>
          <span>{{ layout.name }}</span>
        </button>
      </div>
      
      <div class="view-options">
        <button
          class="view-btn"
          :class="{ active: cardView === 'grid' }"
          @click="cardView = 'grid'"
        >
          <i class="icon-grid"></i>
        </button>
        <button
          class="view-btn"
          :class="{ active: cardView === 'list' }"
          @click="cardView = 'list'"
        >
          <i class="icon-list"></i>
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- å¡ç‰‡ç½‘æ ¼ -->
    <div
      class="cards-container"
      :class="[
        `layout-${currentLayout}`,
        `view-${cardView}`,
        `theme-${currentTheme}`
      ]"
    >
      <template v-if="cardView === 'grid'">
        <!-- ç½‘æ ¼å¸ƒå±€ -->
        <div
          v-for="(row, rowIndex) in gridRows"
          :key="rowIndex"
          class="card-row"
        >
          <div
            v-for="card in row"
            :key="card.id"
            class="card-cell"
            :class="`span-${card.span || 1}`"
          >
            <CardFactory
              :type="card.type"
              :theme="card.theme || currentTheme"
              :data="card.data"
              :config="card.config"
              @action="handleCardAction"
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      </template>
      
      <template v-else>
        <!-- åˆ—è¡¨å¸ƒå±€ -->
        <div class="card-list">
          <div
            v-for="card in cards"
            :key="card.id"
            class="card-list-item"
          >
            <CardFactory
              :type="card.type"
              :theme="card.theme || currentTheme"
              :data="card.data"
              :config="card.config"
              @action="handleCardAction"
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      </template>
    </div>
    
    <!-- ç©ºçŠ¶æ€ -->
    <div v-if="!cards.length" class="empty-state">
      <div class="empty-icon">
        <i class="icon-inbox"></i>
      </div>
      <h3 class="empty-title">æš‚æ— æ•°æ®</h3>
      <p class="empty-description">å½“å‰æ²¡æœ‰å¯æ˜¾ç¤ºçš„å†…å®¹</p>
      <button class="empty-action" @click="handleEmptyAction">
        <i class="icon-plus"></i>
        <span>åˆ›å»ºæ–°å†…å®¹</span>
      </button>
    </div>
    
    <!-- åŠ è½½çŠ¶æ€ -->
    <div v-if="loading" class="loading-state">
      <div class="loading-spinner">
        <div class="spinner-circle"></div>
      </div>
      <p class="loading-text">åŠ è½½ä¸­...</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, computed, onMounted } from 'vue'
import CardFactory from '@/components/cards/CardFactory.vue'

// Props
const props = defineProps({
  cards: {
    type: Array,
    default: () => []
  },
  theme: {
    type: String,
    default: 'system'
  },
  layout: {
    type: String,
    default: 'balanced'
  },
  showControls: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: true
  },
  loading: {
    type: Boolean,
    default: false
  }
})

// Emits
const emit = defineEmits(['action', 'layout-change', 'empty-action'])

// å“åº”å¼æ•°æ®
const currentLayout = ref(props.layout)
const cardView = ref('grid')
const isMounted = ref(false)

// å¸ƒå±€é€‰é¡¹
const layoutOptions = ref([
  {
    id: 'compact',
    name: 'ç´§å‡‘å¸ƒå±€',
    icon: 'icon-layout-compact',
    columns: 4
  },
  {
    id: 'balanced',
    name: 'å¹³è¡¡å¸ƒå±€',
    icon: 'icon-layout-balanced',
    columns: 3
  },
  {
    id: 'spacious',
    name: 'å®½æ¾å¸ƒå±€',
    icon: 'icon-layout-spacious',
    columns: 2
  },
  {
    id: 'focus',
    name: 'ç„¦ç‚¹å¸ƒå±€',
    icon: 'icon-layout-focus',
    columns: 1
  }
])

// è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
const currentTheme = computed(() => props.theme)

const gridRows = computed(() => {
  if (cardView.value !== 'grid') return []
  
  const layout = layoutOptions.value.find(l => l.id === currentLayout.value)
  const columns = layout?.columns || 3
  
  const rows = []
  let currentRow = []
  
  props.cards.forEach((card, index) => {
    const cardSpan = card.span || 1
    
    // å¦‚æœå½“å‰è¡Œæ”¾ä¸ä¸‹è¿™ä¸ªå¡ç‰‡ï¼Œå¼€å§‹æ–°çš„ä¸€è¡Œ
    const currentRowSpan = currentRow.reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c.span || 1), 0)
    if (currentRowSpan + cardSpan > columns) {
      rows.push(currentRow)
      currentRow = [card]
    } else {
      currentRow.push(card)
    }
    
    // å¦‚æœæ˜¯æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªå¡ç‰‡ï¼ŒæŠŠå½“å‰è¡ŒåŠ å…¥rows
    if (index === props.cards.length - 1) {
      rows.push(currentRow)
    }
  })
  
  return rows
})

// æ–¹æ³•
const switchLayout = (layoutId) => {
  currentLayout.value = layoutId
  emit('layout-change', layoutId)
}

const handleCardAction = (action) => {
  emit('action', action)
}

const handleEmptyAction = () => {
  emit('empty-action')
}

// ç”Ÿå‘½å‘¨æœŸ
onMounted(() => {
  isMounted.value = true
})
</script>

<style lang="scss" scoped>
```

## 11.3 å…¨å±€å¼¹çª—è‡ªæ²»ç³»ç»Ÿ

### 11.3.1 å¼¹çª—ç®¡ç†å™¨å®ç°

```typescript
// composables/useModalManager.ts
import { ref, computed, reactive, onUnmounted } from 'vue'

export interface ModalConfig {
  id: string
  component: any
  props?: Record<string, any>
  events?: Record<string, Function>
  options?: ModalOptions
}

export interface ModalOptions {
  title?: string
  width?: string | number
  height?: string | number
  theme?: string
  closable?: boolean
  maskClosable?: boolean
  showClose?: boolean
  showHeader?: boolean
  showFooter?: boolean
  customClass?: string
  zIndex?: number
  animation?: string
  position?: 'center' | 'top' | 'bottom' | 'left' | 'right'
}

export interface ModalInstance {
  id: string
  component: any
  props: Record<string, any>
  events: Record<string, Function>
  options: ModalOptions
  visible: boolean
  zIndex: number
}

class ModalManager {
  private modals = reactive<Map<string, ModalInstance>>(new Map())
  private zIndexBase = 2000
  private activeModals: string[] = []

  // æ‰“å¼€å¼¹çª—
  open(config: ModalConfig): string {
    const { id, component, props = {}, events = {}, options = {} } = config
    
    // å¦‚æœå¼¹çª—å·²å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œå…ˆå…³é—­
    if (this.modals.has(id)) {
      this.close(id)
    }

    const zIndex = this.zIndexBase + this.modals.size
    
    const modalInstance: ModalInstance = {
      id,
      component,
      props,
      events,
      options: {
        theme: 'system',
        closable: true,
        maskClosable: true,
        showClose: true,
        showHeader: true,
        showFooter: false,
        width: '600px',
        position: 'center',
        animation: 'scale',
        ...options
      },
      visible: true,
      zIndex
    }

    this.modals.set(id, modalInstance)
    this.activeModals.push(id)
    
    // é˜»æ­¢èƒŒæ™¯æ»šåŠ¨
    this.updateBodyScroll()
    
    return id
  }

  // å…³é—­å¼¹çª—
  close(id: string): void {
    const modal = this.modals.get(id)
    if (modal) {
      modal.visible = false
      
      // å»¶è¿Ÿç§»é™¤ï¼Œç­‰å¾…åŠ¨ç”»å®Œæˆ
      setTimeout(() => {
        this.modals.delete(id)
        this.activeModals = this.activeModals.filter(modalId => modalId !== id)
        this.updateBodyScroll()
      }, 300)
    }
  }

  // å…³é—­æ‰€æœ‰å¼¹çª—
  closeAll(): void {
    this.modals.forEach(modal => {
      modal.visible = false
    })
    
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.modals.clear()
      this.activeModals = []
      this.updateBodyScroll()
    }, 300)
  }

  // æ›´æ–°å¼¹çª—å±æ€§
  update(id: string, updates: Partial<ModalInstance>): void {
    const modal = this.modals.get(id)
    if (modal) {
      Object.assign(modal, updates)
    }
  }

  // è·å–å¼¹çª—å®ä¾‹
  get(id: string): ModalInstance | undefined {
    return this.modals.get(id)
  }

  // è·å–æ‰€æœ‰å¼¹çª—
  getAll(): ModalInstance[] {
    return Array.from(this.modals.values())
  }

  // è·å–å¯è§å¼¹çª—æ•°é‡
  getVisibleCount(): number {
    return this.activeModals.length
  }

  // æ˜¯å¦æœ‰å¼¹çª—æ˜¾ç¤º
  hasVisible(): boolean {
    return this.activeModals.length > 0
  }

  // æ›´æ–°bodyæ»šåŠ¨çŠ¶æ€
  private updateBodyScroll(): void {
    const hasModals = this.hasVisible()
    document.body.style.overflow = hasModals ? 'hidden' : ''
  }

  // è·å–ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªzIndex
  private getNextZIndex(): number {
    return this.zIndexBase + this.modals.size + 1
  }
}

// å…¨å±€å¼¹çª—ç®¡ç†å™¨å®ä¾‹
const modalManager = new ModalManager()

// Vue composable
export function useModalManager() {
  const modals = computed(() => modalManager.getAll())
  const hasVisibleModals = computed(() => modalManager.hasVisible())
  const visibleCount = computed(() => modalManager.getVisibleCount())

  // æ‰“å¼€å¼¹çª—
  const openModal = (config: ModalConfig): string => {
    return modalManager.open(config)
  }

  // å…³é—­å¼¹çª—
  const closeModal = (id: string): void => {
    modalManager.close(id)
  }

  // å…³é—­æ‰€æœ‰å¼¹çª—
  const closeAllModals = (): void => {
    modalManager.closeAll()
  }

  // æ›´æ–°å¼¹çª—
  const updateModal = (id: string, updates: Partial<ModalInstance>): void => {
    modalManager.update(id, updates)
  }

  // è·å–å¼¹çª—
  const getModal = (id: string): ModalInstance | undefined => {
    return modalManager.get(id)
  }

  // é¢„å®šä¹‰å¼¹çª—ç±»å‹
  const modalTypes = {
    confirm: (config: {
      title?: string
      content: string
      theme?: string
      confirmText?: string
      cancelText?: string
      onConfirm?: () => void
      onCancel?: () => void
    }) => {
      return openModal({
        id: `confirm-${Date.now()}`,
        component: () => import('@/components/modals/ConfirmModal.vue'),
        props: {
          title: config.title || 'ç¡®è®¤æ“ä½œ',
          content: config.content,
          theme: config.theme || 'system',
          confirmText: config.confirmText || 'ç¡®è®¤',
          cancelText: config.cancelText || 'å–æ¶ˆ'
        },
        events: {
          confirm: config.onConfirm,
          cancel: config.onCancel
        },
        options: {
          width: '400px',
          showFooter: true
        }
      })
    },

    alert: (config: {
      title?: string
      content: string
      theme?: string
      buttonText?: string
      onClose?: () => void
    }) => {
      return openModal({
        id: `alert-${Date.now()}`,
        component: () => import('@/components/modals/AlertModal.vue'),
        props: {
          title: config.title || 'æç¤º',
          content: config.content,
          theme: config.theme || 'system',
          buttonText: config.buttonText || 'çŸ¥é“äº†'
        },
        events: {
          close: config.onClose
        },
        options: {
          width: '400px',
          showFooter: true
        }
      })
    },

    form: (config: {
      title: string
      formComponent: any
      formProps?: Record<string, any>
      theme?: string
      width?: string
      onSubmit?: (data: any) => void
      onCancel?: () => void
    }) => {
      return openModal({
        id: `form-${Date.now()}`,
        component: () => import('@/components/modals/FormModal.vue'),
        props: {
          title: config.title,
          formComponent: config.formComponent,
          formProps: config.formProps || {},
          theme: config.theme || 'system'
        },
        events: {
          submit: config.onSubmit,
          cancel: config.onCancel
        },
        options: {
          width: config.width || '600px',
          showFooter: true
        }
      })
    },

    drawer: (config: {
      title?: string
      component: any
      props?: Record<string, any>
      theme?: string
      position?: 'left' | 'right' | 'top' | 'bottom'
      size?: string
      onClose?: () => void
    }) => {
      return openModal({
        id: `drawer-${Date.now()}`,
        component: config.component,
        props: config.props || {},
        events: {
          close: config.onClose
        },
        options: {
          title: config.title,
          theme: config.theme || 'system',
          position: config.position || 'right',
          width: config.size || '400px',
          showHeader: true,
          showClose: true,
          maskClosable: true
        }
      })
    }
  }

  onUnmounted(() => {
    closeAllModals()
  })

  return {
    modals,
    hasVisibleModals,
    visibleCount,
    openModal,
    closeModal,
    closeAllModals,
    updateModal,
    getModal,
    modalTypes
  }
}

```

### 11.3.2 æ™ºèƒ½å¼¹çª—å®¹å™¨

```plaintext
<!-- components/modals/ModalContainer.vue -->
<template>
  <Teleport to="body">
    <transition-group name="modal-fade">
      <div
        v-for="modal in visibleModals"
        :key="modal.id"
        class="modal-overlay"
        :style="{ zIndex: modal.zIndex }"
        @click.self="handleMaskClick(modal)"
      >
        <div
          class="modal-container"
          :class="[
            `theme-${modal.options.theme}`,
            `position-${modal.options.position}`,
            `animation-${modal.options.animation}`,
            modal.options.customClass
          ]"
          :style="modalStyle(modal)"
        >
          <!-- å¼¹çª—å¤´éƒ¨ -->
          <div
            v-if="modal.options.showHeader"
            class="modal-header"
          >
            <div class="header-content">
              <h3 class="modal-title">
                <i
                  v-if="modal.options.theme"
                  :class="themeIcon(modal.options.theme)"
                  class="title-icon"
                ></i>
                {{ modal.options.title }}
              </h3>
              
              <div class="header-actions">
                <button
                  v-if="modal.options.showClose"
                  class="close-btn"
                  @click="closeModal(modal.id)"
                >
                  <i class="icon-close"></i>
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- è¿›åº¦æ¡ -->
            <div
              v-if="modal.props.progress !== undefined"
              class="progress-bar"
            >
              <div
                class="progress-fill"
                :style="{ width: `${modal.props.progress}%` }"
              ></div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- å¼¹çª—å†…å®¹ -->
          <div class="modal-content">
            <component
              :is="modal.component"
              v-bind="modal.props"
              v-on="modal.events"
            />
          </div>
          
          <!-- å¼¹çª—åº•éƒ¨ -->
          <div
            v-if="modal.options.showFooter"
            class="modal-footer"
          >
            <slot name="footer" :modal="modal">
              <div class="footer-actions">
                <button
                  class="btn-secondary"
                  @click="handleCancel(modal)"
                >
                  å–æ¶ˆ
                </button>
                <button
                  class="btn-primary"
                  :class="`theme-${modal.options.theme}`"
                  @click="handleConfirm(modal)"
                >
                  ç¡®è®¤
                </button>
              </div>
            </slot>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </transition-group>
  </Teleport>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { computed } from 'vue'
import { useModalManager } from '@/composables/useModalManager'
import type { ModalInstance } from '@/composables/useModalManager'

const { modals, closeModal } = useModalManager()

// è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
const visibleModals = computed(() => {
  return modals.value.filter(modal => modal.visible)
})

// æ–¹æ³•
const handleMaskClick = (modal: ModalInstance) => {
  if (modal.options.maskClosable && modal.options.closable) {
    closeModal(modal.id)
  }
}

const modalStyle = (modal: ModalInstance) => {
  const style: Record<string, string> = {}
  
  if (modal.options.width) {
    style.width = typeof modal.options.width === 'number' 
      ? `${modal.options.width}px` 
      : modal.options.width
  }
  
  if (modal.options.height) {
    style.height = typeof modal.options.height === 'number'
      ? `${modal.options.height}px`
      : modal.options.height
  }
  
  return style
}

const themeIcon = (theme: string) => {
  const icons: Record<string, string> = {
    menu: 'icon-layout',
    form: 'icon-form',
    knowledge: 'icon-brain',
    ai: 'icon-ai',
    data: 'icon-database',
    system: 'icon-settings'
  }
  return icons[theme] || 'icon-circle'
}

const handleCancel = (modal: ModalInstance) => {
  if (modal.events.cancel) {
    modal.events.cancel()
  }
  closeModal(modal.id)
}

const handleConfirm = (modal: ModalInstance) => {
  if (modal.events.confirm) {
    modal.events.confirm()
  } else {
    closeModal(modal.id)
  }
}
</script>

<style lang="scss" scoped>
@import '@/styles/theme/colors';

  top: 0;

  right: 0;
```

### 11.3.3 é¢„å®šä¹‰å¼¹çª—ç»„ä»¶

```plaintext
<!-- components/modals/ConfirmModal.vue -->
<template>
  <div class="confirm-modal">
    <div class="modal-icon" :class="`theme-${theme}`">
      <i class="icon-help-circle"></i>
    </div>
    
    <div class="modal-content">
      <h3 class="content-title" v-if="title">{{ title }}</h3>
      <div class="content-text">
        {{ content }}
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="modal-actions">
      <button class="btn-cancel" @click="handleCancel">
        {{ cancelText }}
      </button>
      <button class="btn-confirm" :class="`theme-${theme}`" @click="handleConfirm">
        {{ confirmText }}
      </button>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
// Props
const props = defineProps({
  title: String,
  content: {
    type: String,
    required: true
  },
  theme: {
    type: String,
    default: 'system'
  },
  confirmText: {
    type: String,
    default: 'ç¡®è®¤'
  },
  cancelText: {
    type: String,
    default: 'å–æ¶ˆ'
  }
})

// Emits
const emit = defineEmits(['confirm', 'cancel'])

// æ–¹æ³•
const handleConfirm = () => {
  emit('confirm')
}

const handleCancel = () => {
  emit('cancel')
}
</script>
```

```plaintext
<!-- components/modals/FormModal.vue -->
<template>
  <div class="form-modal">
    <div class="form-content">
      <component
        :is="formComponent"
        v-bind="formProps"
        ref="formRef"
        @submit="handleFormSubmit"
        @cancel="handleFormCancel"
      />
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref } from 'vue'

// Props
const props = defineProps({
  formComponent: {
    type: Object,
    required: true
  },
  formProps: {
    type: Object,
    default: () => ({})
  }
})

// Emits
const emit = defineEmits(['submit', 'cancel'])

// æ¨¡æ¿å¼•ç”¨
const formRef = ref()

// æ–¹æ³•
const handleFormSubmit = (formData) => {
  emit('submit', formData)
}

const handleFormCancel = () => {
  emit('cancel')
}

// æš´éœ²æ–¹æ³•ç»™çˆ¶ç»„ä»¶
defineExpose({
  getFormData: () => formRef.value?.getFormData?.(),
  validate: () => formRef.value?.validate?.(),
  reset: () => formRef.value?.reset?.()
})
</script>

<style lang="scss" scoped>
.form-modal {
  .form-content {
    min-height: 200px;
  }
}
</style>

```

### ğŸŒ ç”Ÿæ€åŒ–æ•´åˆä½“ç°

- è®¾è®¡ç³»ç»Ÿï¼šå®Œæ•´çš„è‰²å½©ã€å­—ä½“ã€é—´è·è§„èŒƒ
- ç»„ä»¶ç”Ÿæ€ï¼šå¯å¤ç”¨çš„UIç»„ä»¶åº“
- äº¤äº’æ¨¡å¼ï¼šç»Ÿä¸€çš„ç”¨æˆ·äº¤äº’ä½“éªŒ
è¿™ä¸€UI/UXç³»ç»Ÿä¸ºæ™ºæ¢æœåŠ¡åŒ–å¹³å°æä¾›äº†ç¾è§‚ã€ä¸€è‡´ã€é«˜æ•ˆçš„ç”¨æˆ·ç•Œé¢ï¼Œå®Œå…¨ç¬¦åˆç°ä»£åŒ–ä¼ä¸šçº§åº”ç”¨çš„è®¾è®¡æ ‡å‡†ã€‚

# ç¬¬ä¹ç« ï¼šå®æ–½é£é™©è¯„ä¼°ä¸åº”å¯¹ç­–ç•¥9-12
<https://docs.gtimg.com/docs-design-resources/individuation/desktop/tmoji/book_canvasemoji_80-7049814826.png>
    - å››ä¸ªæ–¹å‘å±•å¼€
        ç»§ç»­æŒ‰ç…§ä¹‹å‰ç¡®è®¤çš„æ¶æ„å’Œè®¾è®¡ç†å¿µï¼Œè¿›è¡Œä¸‹ä¸€æ­¥çš„è¯¦ç»†è®¾è®¡ã€‚æ¥ä¸‹æ¥å°†å›´ç»•ä»¥ä¸‹å››ä¸ªæ–¹å‘å±•å¼€ï¼š
        1. å…·ä½“æŠ€æœ¯é€‰å‹ä¸æ¶æ„ç»†èŠ‚
        1. å„å•å…ƒè¯¦ç»†APIè§„èŒƒ
        1. å®æ–½é£é™©è¯„ä¼°ä¸åº”å¯¹ç­–ç•¥
        1. å›¢é˜Ÿèƒ½åŠ›å»ºè®¾è§„åˆ’
        åŒæ—¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å°†èå…¥æ‚¨å¯¹UIè®¾è®¡çš„å»ºè®®ï¼Œç¡®ä¿å…¨å±€ç»Ÿä¸€æ€§å’Œäº¤äº’å“åº”è®¾è®¡ã€‚

### 11.2 æ™ºèƒ½åŠŸèƒ½å¡ç‰‡ç³»ç»Ÿ

```typescript
<template>
  <div 
    class="smart-card"
    :class="[`card-type-${type}`, `card-size-${size}`]"
    :style="cardStyle"
  >
    <div class="card-header">
      <div class="card-title">
        <i v-if="icon" :class="icon" class="card-icon"></i>
        <h3>{{ title }}</h3>
        <el-tag v-if="tag" :type="tagType" size="small">{{ tag }}</el-tag>
      </div>
      <div class="card-actions">
        <slot name="actions">
          <el-button 
            v-if="showAction" 
            :type="actionType"
            @click="handleAction"
          >
            {{ actionText }}
          </el-button>
        </slot>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="card-content">
      <slot></slot>
    </div>
    
    <div v-if="$slots.footer" class="card-footer">
      <slot name="footer"></slot>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
interface Props {
  type: 'management' | 'operation' | 'monitoring' | 'analysis'
  size?: 'small' | 'medium' | 'large'
  title: string
  icon?: string
  tag?: string
  tagType?: 'success' | 'warning' | 'danger' | 'info'
  showAction?: boolean
  actionText?: string
  actionType?: 'primary' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'danger'
}

const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
  size: 'medium',
  tagType: 'info',
  showAction: false,
  actionText: 'æ“ä½œ',
  actionType: 'primary'
})

const emit = defineEmits<{
  action: []
}>()

const handleAction = () => {
  emit('action')
}

const cardStyle = computed(() => {
  const colorMap = {
    management: 'var(--sm-color-primary)',
    operation: 'var(--sm-color-success)', 
    monitoring: 'var(--sm-color-warning)',
    analysis: 'var(--sm-color-info)'
  }
  return {
    '--card-color': colorMap[props.type]
  }
})
</script>
```

### 11.3 å…¨å±€å¼¹çª—è‡ªæ²»ç³»ç»Ÿ

#### å¼¹çª—ç®¡ç†å™¨å®ç°

```typescript
// composables/useModal.ts
import { ref, reactive, provide, inject, type InjectionKey } from 'vue'

interface ModalConfig {
  id: string
  title: string
  component: any
  props?: Record<string, any>
  width?: string
  customClass?: string
  closeOnClickModal?: boolean
  showClose?: boolean
}

interface ModalInstance {
  id: string
  visible: boolean
  config: ModalConfig
  resolve: (value: any) => void
  reject: (reason?: any) => void
}

const modalSymbol: InjectionKey<ModalManager> = Symbol('modalManager')

class ModalManager {
  private modals = reactive<Map<string, ModalInstance>>(new Map())
  private zIndex = 2000

  show<T>(config: ModalConfig): Promise<T> {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const modalInstance: ModalInstance = {
        id: config.id,
        visible: true,
        config,
        resolve,
        reject
      }
      
      this.modals.set(config.id, modalInstance)
      this.zIndex++
    })
  }

  close(id: string, result?: any) {
    const modal = this.modals.get(id)
    if (modal) {
      modal.visible = false
      modal.resolve(result)
      setTimeout(() => {
        this.modals.delete(id)
      }, 300) // ç­‰å¾…åŠ¨ç”»ç»“æŸ
    }
  }

  getActiveModals() {
    return Array.from(this.modals.values())
  }

  getNextZIndex() {
    return this.zIndex
  }
}

export function useModal() {
  const manager = inject(modalSymbol)
  if (!manager) {
    throw new Error('Modal provider not found')
  }
  return manager
}

export function provideModal() {
  const manager = new ModalManager()
  provide(modalSymbol, manager)
  return manager
}

```

#### æ™ºèƒ½å¼¹çª—å®¹å™¨

```typescript
<template>
  <div class="global-modal-container">
    <div
      v-for="modal in activeModals"
      :key="modal.id"
      class="modal-overlay"
      :style="{ zIndex: getZIndex(modal.id) }"
      @click.self="handleOverlayClick(modal)"
    >
      <div 
        class="modal-content"
        :class="[modal.config.customClass, `modal-type-${getModalType(modal.config)}`]"
        :style="{ width: modal.config.width || '600px' }"
      >
        <div class="modal-header">
          <h3 class="modal-title">{{ modal.config.title }}</h3>
          <div class="modal-actions">
            <el-button
              v-if="modal.config.showClose !== false"
              text
              circle
              @click="closeModal(modal.id)"
            >
              <i class="el-icon-close"></i>
            </el-button>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="modal-body">
          <component
            :is="modal.config.component"
            v-bind="modal.config.props || {}"
            @close="(result: any) => closeModal(modal.id, result)"
            @submit="(result: any) => closeModal(modal.id, result)"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { computed } from 'vue'
import { useModal } from '@/composables/useModal'

const modalManager = useModal()

const activeModals = computed(() => modalManager.getActiveModals())

const getZIndex = (modalId: string) => {
  const baseIndex = 2000
  const index = Array.from(activeModals.value).findIndex(modal => modal.id === modalId)
  return baseIndex + index
}

const getModalType = (config: ModalConfig) => {
  // æ ¹æ®é…ç½®ç¡®å®šå¼¹çª—ç±»å‹ï¼Œç”¨äºæ ·å¼åŒºåˆ†
  return config.customClass?.split('-').pop() || 'default'
}

const handleOverlayClick = (modal: ModalInstance) => {
  if (modal.config.closeOnClickModal !== false) {
    modalManager.close(modal.id)
  }
}

const closeModal = (modalId: string, result?: any) => {
  modalManager.close(modalId, result)
}
</script>

<style scoped>
.modal-overlay {
  position: fixed;
  top: 0;
  left: 0;
  right: 0;
  bottom: 0;
  background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.45);
  backdrop-filter: blur(4px);
  display: flex;
  align-items: center;
  justify-content: center;
  animation: fadeIn 0.3s ease;
}

.modal-content {
  background: #fff;
  border-radius: 8px;
  box-shadow: 0 8px 32px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.12);
  animation: slideIn 0.3s ease;
  max-height: 80vh;
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  
  &.modal-type-primary {
    border-top: 4px solid var(--sm-color-primary);
  }
  
  &.modal-type-success {
    border-top: 4px solid var(--sm-color-success);
  }
  
  &.modal-type-warning {
    border-top: 4px solid var(--sm-color-warning);
  }
  
  &.modal-type-danger {
    border-top: 4px solid var(--sm-color-danger);
  }
}

.modal-header {
  display: flex;
  justify-content: space-between;
  align-items: center;
  padding: 16px 20px;
  border-bottom: 1px solid #f0f0f0;
}

.modal-title {
  margin: 0;
  font-size: 16px;
  font-weight: 600;
}

.modal-body {
  flex: 1;
  padding: 20px;
  overflow-y: auto;
}

@keyframes fadeIn {
  from { opacity: 0; }
  to { opacity: 1; }
}

@keyframes slideIn {
  from {
    opacity: 0;
    transform: translateY(-20px) scale(0.95);
  }
  to {
    opacity: 1;
    transform: translateY(0) scale(1);
  }
}
</style>

```

## ç¬¬åä¸‰ç« ï¼šä¸‹ä¸€æ­¥è¡ŒåŠ¨å®æ–½è§„åˆ’

```typescript
// ç»Ÿä¸€èº«ä»½è®¤è¯æœåŠ¡
class AuthService {
  async authenticate(user: LoginRequest): Promise<AuthResult> {
    // å¤šå› å­è®¤è¯
    if (await this.needMFA(user)) {
      return this.mfaChallenge(user);
    }
    
    // JWTä»¤ç‰Œç­¾å‘
    const token = await this.issueJWT(user);
    
    // ä¼šè¯ç®¡ç†
    await this.createSession(user, token);
    
    return { success: true, token };
  }
  
  // æƒé™éªŒè¯
  async authorize(user: User, resource: string, action: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const permissions = await this.getUserPermissions(user);
    return permissions.some(p => 
      p.resource === resource && p.actions.includes(action)
    );
  }
}

```

```python
class SecurityMonitor:
    def __init__(self):
        self.threat_intelligence = ThreatIntelligenceFeed()
        self.anomaly_detector = AnomalyDetectionModel()
    
    def monitor_security_events(self):
        # å®æ—¶ç›‘æ§å®‰å…¨äº‹ä»¶
        events = self.collect_security_events()
        suspicious_events = self.detect_suspicious_patterns(events)
        
        for event in suspicious_events:
            risk_level = self.assess_risk_level(event)
            if risk_level > self.threshold:
                self.trigger_incident_response(event)
    
    def detect_suspicious_patterns(self, events):
        # åŸºäºæœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ çš„å¼‚å¸¸æ£€æµ‹
        patterns = self.anomaly_detector.predict(events)
        return [event for event, pattern in zip(events, patterns) if pattern.is_anomaly]

```

```sql
-- æ™ºèƒ½ç´¢å¼•ç­–ç•¥
CREATE INDEX idx_menu_restaurant_time 
ON menus(restaurant_id, created_time DESC);

-- æŸ¥è¯¢ä¼˜åŒ–ç¤ºä¾‹
EXPLAIN ANALYZE 
SELECT m.*, COUNT(o.id) as order_count
FROM menus m
LEFT JOIN orders o ON m.id = o.menu_id
WHERE m.restaurant_id = $1
  AND m.status = 'active'
  AND m.created_time > NOW() - INTERVAL '7 days'
GROUP BY m.id
ORDER BY order_count DESC
LIMIT 20;

```

```java
@Service
public class AsyncOrderProcessor {
    
    @Async("orderProcessorExecutor")
    public CompletableFuture<OrderResult> processOrder(Order order) {
        // å¼‚æ­¥è®¢å•å¤„ç†
        return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(process(order));
    }
    
    @Bean("orderProcessorExecutor")
    public TaskExecutor orderProcessorExecutor() {
        ThreadPoolTaskExecutor executor = new ThreadPoolTaskExecutor();
        executor.setCorePoolSize(10);
        executor.setMaxPoolSize(50);
        executor.setQueueCapacity(1000);
        executor.setThreadNamePrefix("order-processor-");
        executor.setRejectedExecutionHandler(new ThreadPoolExecutor.CallerRunsPolicy());
        executor.initialize();
        return executor;
    }
}

```

```python
class PerformanceOptimizer:
    def __init__(self):
        self.metrics_collector = MetricsCollector()
        self.optimization_engine = OptimizationEngine()
    
    def continuous_optimization(self):
        while True:
            # æ”¶é›†æ€§èƒ½æŒ‡æ ‡
            metrics = self.metrics_collector.collect()
            
            # åˆ†ææ€§èƒ½ç“¶é¢ˆ
            bottlenecks = self.analyze_bottlenecks(metrics)
            
            # æ‰§è¡Œä¼˜åŒ–ç­–ç•¥
            for bottleneck in bottlenecks:
                optimization = self.optimization_engine.generate_optimization(bottleneck)
                self.apply_optimization(optimization)
            
            time.sleep(300)  # 5åˆ†é’Ÿæ‰§è¡Œä¸€æ¬¡
    
    def analyze_bottlenecks(self, metrics):
        bottlenecks = []
        
        # æ•°æ®åº“æŸ¥è¯¢åˆ†æ
        if metrics.database.query_time_p95 > 100:  # 100ms
            bottlenecks.append({
                'type': 'database',
                'metric': 'query_time',
                'value': metrics.database.query_time_p95
            })
        
        # APIå“åº”æ—¶é—´åˆ†æ
        if metrics.api.response_time_p95 > 200:  # 200ms
            bottlenecks.append({
                'type': 'api',
                'metric': 'response_time', 
                'value': metrics.api.response_time_p95
            })
        
        return bottlenecks

```

```python
class DataAssessment:
    def analyze_source_data(self):
        analysis = {
            'data_volume': self.calculate_data_volume(),
            'data_quality': self.assess_data_quality(),
            'data_complexity': self.analyze_complexity(),
            'migration_risks': self.identify_risks()
        }
        return analysis
    
    def calculate_data_volume(self):
        # è®¡ç®—å„è¡¨æ•°æ®é‡
        tables = ['users', 'menus', 'orders', 'payments']
        volumes = {}
        for table in tables:
            count = self.get_table_count(table)
            size = self.get_table_size(table)
            volumes[table] = {'count': count, 'size': size}
        return volumes
    
    def assess_data_quality(self):
        # æ•°æ®è´¨é‡è¯„ä¼°
        quality_metrics = {
            'completeness': self.check_completeness(),
            'consistency': self.check_consistency(),
            'accuracy': self.check_accuracy(),
            'uniqueness': self.check_uniqueness()
        }
        return quality_metrics

```

#### ç¬¬äºŒé˜¶æ®µï¼šåŒå†™å®æ–½ï¼ˆ2å‘¨ï¼‰

```java
@Component
public class DualWriteService {
    
    @Async
    @Transactional
    public void dualWrite(String operation, Object data) {
        try {
            // å†™å…¥æ–°ç³»ç»Ÿ
            newSystemService.write(operation, data);
            
            // å†™å…¥æ—§ç³»ç»Ÿ
            oldSystemService.write(operation, data);
            
        } catch (Exception e) {
            // åŒå†™å¤±è´¥å¤„ç†
            handleDualWriteFailure(operation, data, e);
        }
    }
    
    private void handleDualWriteFailure(String operation, Object data, Exception e) {
        // è®°å½•å¤±è´¥æ—¥å¿—
        log.error("Dual write failed for operation: {}", operation, e);
        
        // å‘Šè­¦é€šçŸ¥
        alertService.sendAlert("åŒå†™å¤±è´¥", operation, e.getMessage());
        
        // æ ¹æ®ç­–ç•¥å¤„ç†ï¼šé‡è¯•ã€è¡¥å¿ã€äººå·¥å¹²é¢„
        recoveryService.handleFailure(operation, data, e);
    }
}

```

#### ç¬¬ä¸‰é˜¶æ®µï¼šæ•°æ®éªŒè¯ä¸ä¿®å¤ï¼ˆ1å‘¨ï¼‰

```python
class DataValidator:
    def validate_migration(self):
        validation_results = {}
        
        # æ•°é‡ä¸€è‡´æ€§éªŒè¯
        validation_results['count_consistency'] = self.validate_counts()
        
        # æ•°æ®å†…å®¹éªŒè¯
        validation_results['content_consistency'] = self.validate_content()
        
        # ä¸šåŠ¡é€»è¾‘éªŒè¯
        validation_results['business_logic'] = self.validate_business_logic()
        
        return validation_results
    
    def validate_counts(self):
        tables = ['users', 'menus', 'orders']
        results = {}
        
        for table in tables:
            old_count = self.get_old_system_count(table)
            new_count = self.get_new_system_count(table)
            results[table] = {
                'old_count': old_count,
                'new_count': new_count,
                'match': old_count == new_count
            }
        
        return results
    
    def validate_content(self):
        # æŠ½æ ·æ•°æ®å†…å®¹éªŒè¯
        sample_size = 1000
        samples = self.get_data_samples(sample_size)
        
        mismatches = []
        for sample in samples:
            old_data = self.get_old_system_record(sample.id)
            new_data = self.get_new_system_record(sample.id)
            
            if not self.compare_records(old_data, new_data):
                mismatches.append({
                    'id': sample.id,
                    'old_data': old_data,
                    'new_data': new_data
                })
        
        return {
            'sample_size': sample_size,
            'mismatches': mismatches,
            'accuracy_rate': (sample_size - len(mismatches)) / sample_size
        }

```

#### æ™ºèƒ½æµé‡è°ƒåº¦

```java
@Service
public class TrafficManagementService {
    
    public boolean shouldRouteToNewVersion(User user) {
        // åŸºäºç”¨æˆ·ç‰¹å¾çš„æµé‡è°ƒåº¦
        List<RoutingRule> rules = getRoutingRules();
        
        for (RoutingRule rule : rules) {
            if (rule.matches(user)) {
                return rule.getTargetVersion().equals("v2");
            }
        }
        
        // é»˜è®¤è·¯ç”±åˆ°ç¨³å®šç‰ˆæœ¬
        return false;
    }
    
    private List<RoutingRule> getRoutingRules() {
        return Arrays.asList(
            // å†…éƒ¨å‘˜å·¥è§„åˆ™
            new RoutingRule()
                .userGroup("internal")
                .percentage(100)
                .targetVersion("v2"),
                
            // ç§å­ç”¨æˆ·è§„åˆ™  
            new RoutingRule()
                .userGroup("seed")
                .percentage(100)
                .targetVersion("v2"),
                
            // æ™®é€šç”¨æˆ·è§„åˆ™
            new RoutingRule()
                .userGroup("general") 
                .percentage(30)
                .targetVersion("v2")
        );
    }
}
```

```python
class AutoHealingSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.alert_manager = AlertManager()
        self.recovery_actions = RecoveryActions()
    
    def handle_incident(self, incident):
        # è‡ªåŠ¨è¯Šæ–­æ ¹æœ¬åŸå› 
        root_cause = self.diagnose_root_cause(incident)
        
        # æ‰§è¡Œè‡ªæ„ˆåŠ¨ä½œ
        if root_cause == 'high_cpu_usage':
            self.recovery_actions.scale_out(incident.service)
            
        elif root_cause == 'memory_leak':
            self.recovery_actions.restart_pod(incident.service)
            
        elif root_cause == 'database_slow_queries':
            self.recovery_actions.kill_slow_queries()
            
        else:
            # æ— æ³•è‡ªåŠ¨æ¢å¤ï¼Œå‡çº§åˆ°äººå·¥å¤„ç†
            self.alert_manager.escalate_to_human(incident)
    
    def diagnose_root_cause(self, incident):
        # åŸºäºæœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ çš„åŸå› åˆ†æ
        features = self.extract_features(incident)
        return self.ml_model.predict(features)

```

```python
class CapacityPlanner:
    def __init__(self):
        self.historical_data = HistoricalDataLoader()
        self.forecast_model = ForecastModel()
    
    def predict_capacity_needs(self, horizon_days=30):
        # åŸºäºå†å²æ•°æ®é¢„æµ‹
        historical_metrics = self.historical_data.load_metrics()
        
        predictions = {}
        for metric in ['cpu_usage', 'memory_usage', 'storage_usage']:
            prediction = self.forecast_model.predict(
                historical_metrics[metric], 
                horizon_days
            )
            predictions[metric] = prediction
        
        # ç”Ÿæˆæ‰©å®¹å»ºè®®
        recommendations = self.generate_recommendations(predictions)
        return predictions, recommendations
    
    def generate_recommendations(self, predictions):
        recommendations = []
        
        if predictions['cpu_usage'].max() > 0.8:  # 80%é˜ˆå€¼
            recommendations.append({
                'action': 'scale_cpu',
                'reason': 'CPUä½¿ç”¨ç‡é¢„æµ‹è¶…è¿‡é˜ˆå€¼',
                'timeline': '2å‘¨å†…'
            })
        
        if predictions['storage_usage'].max() > 0.85:  # 85%é˜ˆå€¼
            recommendations.append({
                'action': 'expand_storage',
                'reason': 'å­˜å‚¨ä½¿ç”¨ç‡é¢„æµ‹è¶…è¿‡é˜ˆå€¼', 
                'timeline': '1ä¸ªæœˆå†…'
            })
        
        return recommendations

```

```java
        // 1. éœ€æ±‚é¢„æµ‹å…±äº«
        shareDemandForecastWithSuppliers();
        
        // 2. åº“å­˜å¯è§†åŒ–ç®¡ç†
```

```python
class FinancialAIDecisionEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.cost_optimizer = CostOptimizer()
        self.investment_analyzer = InvestmentAnalyzer()
        self.risk_assessor = RiskAssessor()
    
    def make_financial_decisions(self, business_context):
        decisions = {}
        
        # æˆæœ¬ä¼˜åŒ–å†³ç­–
        cost_opportunities = self.cost_optimizer.identify_opportunities()
        decisions['cost_optimization'] = self.prioritize_cost_actions(cost_opportunities)
        
        # æŠ•èµ„å†³ç­–
        investment_options = self.investment_analyzer.evaluate_options()
        decisions['investment_recommendations'] = self.rank_investments(investment_options)
        
        # é£é™©ç®¡ç†å†³ç­–
        risk_mitigation = self.risk_assessor.assess_mitigation_strategies()
        decisions['risk_management'] = self.select_risk_strategies(risk_mitigation)
        
        return decisions
    
    def generate_financial_insights(self):
        # è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆè´¢åŠ¡æ´å¯ŸæŠ¥å‘Š
        insights = {
            'profitability_drivers': self.analyze_profitability_drivers(),
            'cost_structure_optimization': self.optimize_cost_structure(),
            'working_capital_efficiency': self.assess_working_capital(),
            'investment_roi_analysis': self.calculate_investment_roi()
        }
        return insights

```
